class="wp-block-group alignfull has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained" style=padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><h1 class="wp-block-post-title">Volunteer &#8211; Human Genomics – 2 Positions (No Experience NGO Jobs) Jobs – Infectious Diseases Institute (IDI)</h1><div
class="wp-block-group has-link-color has-accent-4-color has-text-color has-small-font-size is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-4efaea1e wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style=margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><p>This job falls under:</p><div
style=font-weight:300 class="taxonomy-category wp-block-post-terms"><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/communications-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Communications Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/health-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Health Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/information-technology-it-and-data-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Information Technology (IT) and Data Jobs in Uganda</a></div></div><div
class="entry-content alignfull wp-block-post-content has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-post-content-is-layout-constrained"><div
class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; background-color: FFFFFF;'><div
align=center> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script> 
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=7510899927
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div></div><p><strong>Job Title: </strong><a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ ><strong> Volunteer &#8211; Human Genomics – 2 Positions (No Experience NGO Jobs)  </strong></a></p><p><strong>Organisation: </strong>Infectious Diseases Institute (IDI)</p><p><strong>Duty Station:</strong> Kampala, Uganda</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>About Organisation:</strong></p><p>Infectious Diseases Institute (IDI) is an independently governed institute within the College of Health Sciences at Makerere University and has the mission “To strengthen health systems in Africa, with a strong emphasis on infectious diseases, through research and capacity development.” IDI has operations across Uganda as well as in a number of other African countries and has a staffing of over 1,000 managing multiple projects in research, clinical services, public health and training.</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>Job Summary: </strong> The African Center of Excellence in Bioinformatics and Data-Intensive Sciences (ACE) Uganda is offering two (2) internship opportunities supported by the SHEDS project in partnership with the Institute for Global Health Sciences (IGHS), University of California San Francisco (UCSF). Interns will participate in real-world, data-driven health research projects while building practical skills.</p><p></p><p><strong>Key Duties and Responsibilities: </strong></p><ul>
<li>Learning how to program in any of the following languages: R, Python, Bash scripting</li>
<li>Cleaning, analyzing, and visualizing health data using R, Python, or Bash scripting.</li>
<li>Using bioinformatics tools to align DNA sequences, identify genetic variants or perform basic statistical analysis on genomic data.</li>
<li>Developing pipelines for bioinformatics analysis.</li>
<li>Reviewing and summarizing relevant literature to inform project activities.</li>
<li>Participating in team meetings and delivering presentations on progress.</li>
<li>Submitting monthly progress reports and a final internship report.</li>
<li>Contributing to ongoing ACE projects.</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>Qualifications, Skills and Experience:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><ul>
<li>Bachelor’s degree in Biochemistry, Biomedical Laboratory Technology, Biotechnology or a related field.</li></ul><p><strong><em>Person Specification</em></strong></p><ul>
<li>A recent graduate (within the last year) with a Bachelor’s degree in Biochemistry, Biomedical Laboratory Technology, Biotechnology or a related field from a recognized university.</li>
<li>Demonstrated interest in the application of health data science or bioinformatics or structural biology in human genomics.</li>
<li>Willingness to learn and contribute in a multidisciplinary environment.</li>
<li>Plans to pursue a career in health data science or a related field.</li>
<li>Strong written and verbal communication skills.</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>How to Apply:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><p>Submit a single PDF document including:</p><ul>
<li>Certified academic transcripts or a stamped testimonial if pending graduation.</li>
<li>Copy of UACE results.</li>
<li>Two reference letters on institutional letterhead from academic referees.</li>
<li>Cover page (max 1500 words) outlining:</li>
<li>A general introduction about yourself e.g. student, recent graduate and field of study.</li>
<li>The area you are applying for (human genomics).</li>
<li>Any relevant experience in the area of human genomics.</li>
<li>A one-page research idea aligned with the application of health data science or bioinformatics or structural biology in human genomics.</li>
<li>Updated CV (maximum 3 pages)</li></ul><p></p><p><a
href=https://idi.mak.ac.ug/opportunities/home/selected_job/2244 rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank><strong>Click Here</strong></a></p><p></p><p>Note: Only shortlisted candidates will be contacted. We will only accept one application per individual.</p><p></p><p><strong>Deadline: 19th September 2025</strong></p><p></p><p></p><p>For more of the latest jobs, please visit <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ >https://www.theugandanjobline.com</a> or find us on our facebook page <a
href=https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank>https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline</a></p><p><strong> </strong></p><p></p><p><strong>Level of Education: Bachelor Degree</strong></p><p><strong>Work Hours: 8</strong></p><p><strong>Experience in Months: no experience required </strong></p><p><script type=application/ld+json>{"@context":"https://schema.org/","@type":"JobPosting","title":"Volunteer - Human Genomics \u2013 2 Positions - Kampala","description":"Job Summary:   The African Center of Excellence in Bioinformatics and Data-Intensive Sciences (ACE) Uganda is offering two (2) internship opportunities supported by the SHEDS project in partnership with the Institute for Global Health Sciences (IGHS), University of California San Francisco (UCSF). class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-28f84493 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex"><div
class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style=flex-basis:66.66%><div
class="wp-block-group alignfull has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained" style=padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><h1 class="wp-block-post-title">Management Accountant Jobs – Uganda National Oil Company (UNOC)</h1><div
class="wp-block-group has-link-color has-accent-4-color has-text-color has-small-font-size is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-4efaea1e wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style=margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><p>This job falls under:</p><div
style=font-weight:300 class="taxonomy-category wp-block-post-terms"><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/government-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Government Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/oil-petroleum-and-gas-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Oil Petroleum and Gas Jobs in Uganda</a></div></div><div
class="entry-content alignfull wp-block-post-content has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-post-content-is-layout-constrained"><div
class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; background-color: FFFFFF;'><div
align=center> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script> 
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=7510899927
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div></div><p><strong>Job Title: </strong><a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com><strong> Management Accountant  </strong></a></p><p><strong>Organisation:</strong> Uganda National Oil Company (UNOC)</p><p><strong>Duty Station:</strong>  Kampala, Uganda</p><p><strong>Reports to:</strong> Senior Management Accountant</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>About Organisation:</strong></p><p>The Uganda National Oil Company (UNOC) Ltd was established under the Petroleum (Exploration, Development and Production) Act and the Petroleum (Refining, Conversion, Transmission and Midstream storage) Act, both of 2013 and incorporated under the Companies&#8217; Act, 2012. It is a limited liability company wholly owned by the Government of Uganda. The overall function of UNOC is to handle the State&#8217;s commercial interests in the Oil and Gas industry and ensure that the resource is exploited in a sustainable manner.</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>Job Summary: </strong> To facilitate decision making through provision of relevant information to senior management of unoc such as timely management accounting reports, data on business performance against budget, effective cost accounting system, effective budgetary controls systems, internal control procedures</p><p></p><p><strong>Key Duties and Responsibilities: </strong></p><ul>
<li>Prepare variance reports for each department and make appropriate.</li>
<li>recommendations on budgetary performance/department expenses.</li>
<li>Participate in the preparation and review of the Government planning documents such as Budget Framework Paper, Ministerial Policy Statement, National</li>
<li>Development Plan II among others and providing resulting insights to the CFO for decision making.</li>
<li>Participate in the development of quarterly and annual work plans for UNOC and its subsidiaries.</li>
<li>Participate in the review of departmental work plans and budgets for the joint venture partners of UNOC and its subsidiaries.</li>
<li>Coordinate and prepare management accounts monthly.</li>
<li>Regularly review the general ledgers to ensure that balances held are accurate.</li>
<li>Carry out Cost Benefit Analyses of UNOC projects as well as other financial evaluations.</li>
<li>Participate in the creation and evaluation of business strategies to generate shareholder value. </li>
<li>Participate in the budget rationalisation process as required by Ministry Finance, Planning &amp; Economic Development.</li>
<li>Undertake any other duties and responsibilities as may be assigned from time to time by the supervisor(s).</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>Qualifications, Skills and Experience:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><ul>
<li>Bachelors Degree (Hons) in Commerce, Finance, Business Administration, Accounting, Economics or other related fields from a recognised University.</li>
<li>Possession of at least Level II of Accountancy Professional Membership (ACCA / CPA)</li>
<li>A minimum of four (4) years of experience in a finance/budgeting/accounting profession, from a busy and reputable company.</li></ul><p><strong><em>Skills and Competencies</em></strong></p><ul>
<li>Excellent Analytical skills</li>
<li>Attention to detail</li>
<li>High degree of professionalism</li>
<li>Ability to maintain confidentiality</li>
<li>Excellent interpersonal skills and ability to interact with colleagues from all</li>
<li>departments and levels of the organization</li>
<li>Financial Planning &amp; Budgeting</li>
<li>Financial Accounting &amp; Controls</li>
<li>Financial Reporting</li>
<li>Commercial Acumen</li>
<li>Stakeholder Management</li>
<li>Coordination &amp; Planning</li>
<li>Strong communication &amp; Engagement Skills</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>How to Apply:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p></strong></p><p>All interested candidates should submit their applications through the UNOC online recruitment system accessible through this link</p><p> </p><p></p><p><a
href=https://careers.unoc.co.ug/ rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank><strong>Click Here</strong></a></p><p></p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>Deadline: 29th August 2025</strong></p><p></p><p> </p><p><strong>Note:</strong></p><ul>
<li>Only applications routed through the stated link shall be considered.</li>
<li>Any form of canvassing shall lead to automatic disqualification.</li>
<li>UNOC is an equal opportunity employer.</li></ul><p> </p><p></p><p>For more of the latest jobs, please visit <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ >https://www.theugandanjobline.com</a> or find us on our facebook page <a
href=https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank>https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline</a></p><p> </p><p></p><p>Level of Education: Bachelor Degree</p><p>Work Hours: 8</p><p>Experience in Months: 48</p><p><script type=application/ld+json>{"@context":"https://schema.org/","@type":"JobPosting","title":"Management Accountant - Kampala","description":"Job Summary:   To facilitate decision making through provision of relevant information to senior management of unoc such as timely management accounting reports, data on business performance against budget, effective cost accounting system, effective budgetary controls systems, internal control procedures\n\nKey Duties and Responsibilities:  \nPrepare variance reports for each department and make appropriate.recommendations on budgetary performance/department expenses.Participate in the preparation and review of the Government planning documents such as Budget Framework Paper, Ministerial Policy Statement, NationalDevelopment Plan II among others and providing resulting insights to the CFO for decision making.Participate in the development of quarterly and annual work plans for UNOC and its subsidiaries.Participate in the review of departmental work plans and budgets for the joint venture partners of UNOC and its subsidiaries.Coordinate and prepare management accounts monthly.Regularly review the general ledgers to ensure that balances held are accurate.Carry out Cost Benefit Analyses of UNOC projects as well as other financial evaluations.Participate in the creation and evaluation of business strategies to generate shareholder value.\u2003Participate in the budget rationalisation process as required by Ministry Finance, Planning &amp; class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style=flex-basis:66.66%><div
class="wp-block-group alignfull has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained" style=padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><h1 class="wp-block-post-title">Qatar Airways Customer Service Jobs &#8211; Reservations &#038; Ticketing Agent</h1><div
class="wp-block-group has-link-color has-accent-4-color has-text-color has-small-font-size is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-4efaea1e wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style=margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><p>This job falls under:</p><div
style=font-weight:300 class="taxonomy-category wp-block-post-terms"><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/aviation-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Aviation Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/business-administration-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Business Administration Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/customer-service-jobs rel=tag>Customer Service Jobs</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/finance-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Finance Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/sales-and-marketing-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Sales and Marketing Jobs in Uganda</a></div></div><div
class="entry-content alignfull wp-block-post-content has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-post-content-is-layout-constrained"><div
class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; background-color: FFFFFF;'><div
align=center> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script> 
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=7510899927
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div></div><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Job Title:    <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ > Reservations &amp; Ticketing Agent- Entebbe </a></strong></p><p><strong>Organisation:</strong> Qatar Airways (QA)</p><p><strong>Duty Station:</strong> Entebbe, Uganda</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>About Qatar Airways:</strong></p><p>Qatar Airways is the state-owned flag carrier of Qatar and it’s headquartered in the Qatar Airways Tower in Doha<a
href=https://www.blogger.com/blog/post/edit/5878136938400860152/6362547619431128481 rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank>.</a> The airline operates a hub-and-spoke network, linking over 150 international destinations across Africa, Central Asia, Europe, Far East, South Asia, Middle East, North America, South America and Oceania from its base at Hamad International Airport, using a fleet of more than 180 aircraft. Qatar Airways Group employs more than 40,000 people, of whom 24,000 work directly for Qatar Airways. The carrier has been a member of the Oneworld alliance since October 2013, the first Gulf carrier to sign with one of the three airline alliances.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Job Summary: </strong>  We are currently recruiting Reservations and Ticketing Agent for Entebbe, Uganda. In this role you are expected to provide a full service-oriented professional reservations and ticketing service to all customers and travel businesses either through telephone calls or in person meetings in order to achieve optimal customer satisfaction and achieve annual budget revenue targets.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Key Duties and Responsibilities: </strong></p><ul>
<li>Make and confirm reservations for passengers.</li>
<li>Arrange Reservations and routing using timetables, airline manuals, reference guides, and tariff book and proper issuance of ATB for all types of ticketing transactions.</li>
<li>Assist mishandled passengers such as NOREC/DNB to reduce passenger complaints.</li>
<li>Issue tickets quoting correct fare to reduce passenger complaints and debit notes.</li>
<li>Advice on changes in flight plan or to cancel or confirm reservation.</li>
<li>Advice load control personnel and other stations on changes in passenger itinerary to control space and ensure utilization of seating capacity on flights.</li>
<li>Ensure that the sales report is closed on time.</li>
<li>Initiate and promote QR product to generate the revenue.</li>
<li>Record and process reservations made by phone/fax/e-mail; actions telex messages and authorities.</li>
<li>Handle Help desk – assist travel agents with seat confirmations, upgrade/downgrade proposals.</li>
<li>Issuance of MCO’s and refunds; process lost tickets and time barred tickets.</li>
<li>Examine passenger ticket to direct/advise passenger correctly.</li>
<li>Plan route and compute ticket cost, using schedules, rate books, and computer.</li>
<li>Determines whether space is available on travel dates requested by customer.</li>
<li>Telephone customer or Travel Agent to advise of changes with travel conveyance or to confirm reservation, as well as alternate available options.</li>
<li>Sell and assemble tickets for transmittal or mailing to customers.</li>
<li>Answer inquires made by travel agencies or transportation firms, such as airlines, bus companies, railroad companies, and steamship lines.</li>
<li>Be part of an extraordinary story</li>
<li>Your skills. Your imagination. Your ambition. Here, there are no boundaries to your potential and the impact you can make. You’ll find infinite opportunities to grow and work on the biggest, most rewarding challenges that will build your skills and experience. You have the chance to be a part of our future, and build the life you want while being part of an international community. Our best is here and still to come. To us, impossible is only a challenge. Join us as we dare to achieve what’s never been done before. Together, everything is possible.</li></ul><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Qualifications, Skills and Experience: </strong></p><div
style="text-align: center; margin: 20px 0;"><script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458" crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle style="display: block;" data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458 data-ad-slot=9585539503 data-ad-format=auto data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script></div><p>To be successful in this role you will need.</p><ul>
<li>With 3 years of job-related experience/ working as counter staff in the travel agents or airline is mandatory</li>
<li>Recognized IATA / Airline Basic Tariff Course will be an added advantage.</li>
<li>Fair knowledge of World Geography.</li>
<li>Excellent English language communication skills – spoken/written.</li>
<li>Thorough knowledge of special rates/ offers / promotions.</li>
<li>Proven ability to manage room sales with due regard to the Revenue.</li>
<li>Ability to adhere to Management policy and target sales mix to achieve maximum room revenue, ensuring every opportunity to sell is taken.</li>
<li>Demonstrate Quality Consciousness.</li>
<li>Has legal right to live and work in Uganda.</li></ul><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>How to Apply:</strong><br>
If you have what it takes to be part of our 5-star team, please take the first step and apply now by uploading your CV and completing the Qatar Airways online application at the link below.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><a
href=https://careers.qatarairways.com/global/JobDetail/Reservations-Ticketing-Agent-Entebbe-Uganda/72908 rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank><strong>Click Here</strong></a></p><p><strong> </strong></p><p><strong>Deadline: 8th September 2025</strong></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>For more of the latest jobs, please visit <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ >https://www.theugandanjobline.com</a> or find us on our facebook page <a
href=https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank>https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline</a></p><div

class="wp-block-group has-link-color has-accent-4-color has-text-color has-small-font-size is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-4efaea1e wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style=margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><p>This job falls under:</p><div
style=font-weight:300 class="taxonomy-category wp-block-post-terms"><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/communications-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Communications Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/information-technology-it-and-data-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Information Technology (IT) and Data Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/sales-and-marketing-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Sales and Marketing Jobs in Uganda</a></div></div><div
class="entry-content alignfull wp-block-post-content has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-post-content-is-layout-constrained"><div
class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; background-color: FFFFFF;'><div
align=center> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script> 
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=7510899927
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div></div><p><strong>Job Title: </strong><a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ ><strong> Human Resources Coordinator (Pre-Opening)</strong></a></p><p><strong>Organisation: </strong>Marriott International</p><p><strong>Duty Station: </strong>Kampala, Uganda</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>About Organisation:</strong></p><p>Marriott International is the largest hotel company in the world by the number of available rooms. Marriott is an American multinational company that operates, franchises, and licenses lodging brands that include hotel, residential, and timeshare properties. Marriott International owns over 30 hotel and timeshare brands with 8,785 locations and 1,597,380 rooms across its network. Marriott International is headquartered in Bethesda, Maryland. The company is the successor to the hospitality division of the Marriott Corporation, founded by J. Willard Marriott (1900–1985) and his wife Alice Marriott (1907–2000).</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>Key Duties and Responsibilities: </strong></p><ul>
<li>Create and maintain filing systems. </li>
<li>Create and type office correspondence using a computer. </li>
<li>Distribute and route mail. Order and track Human Resources office supplies and forms. </li>
<li>Answer phone calls and record messages. HR Admin. </li>
<li>Support payroll process. </li>
<li>Create new employee personnel file. </li>
<li>Assist walk-in candidates with application procedures. </li>
<li>Maintain space designated for completing applications and ensure it is clean, well maintained, and accessible to individuals with disabilities. </li>
<li>Respond to questions, requests, and concerns from employees and management regarding company and Human Resources programs, policies and guidelines. </li>
<li>Inform Human Resources management of issues related to employee relations within the division or property. </li>
<li>Maintain confidentiality and security of employee and property records, files, and information. </li>
<li>Ensure accurate maintenance of all employee records and files (e.g., interview documents, I-9&#8217;s).</li>
<li>Follow all company policies and procedures; ensure uniform and personal appearance are clean and professional; maintain confidentiality of proprietary information; protect company assets. </li>
<li>Report accidents, injuries, and unsafe work conditions to manager. </li>
<li>Welcome and acknowledge all guests according to company standards. </li>
<li>Speak with others using clear and professional language; prepare and review written documents accurately and completely; answer telephones using appropriate etiquette. </li>
<li>Develop and maintain positive working relationships with others; support team to reach common goals; listen and respond appropriately to the concerns of other employees. </li>
<li>Ensure adherence to quality expectations and standards. </li>
<li>Enter and locate work-related information using computers and/or point of sale systems. </li>
<li>Move, lift, carry, push, pull, and place objects weighing less than or equal to 10 pounds without assistance. </li>
<li>Perform other reasonable job duties as requested by Supervisors.</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>Qualifications, Skills and Experience:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><ul>
<li>Education: High school diploma or G.E.D. equivalent.</li>
<li>Related Work Experience: At least 1 year of related work experience.</li>
<li>Supervisory Experience: No supervisory experience.</li>

class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-28f84493 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex"><div
class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style=flex-basis:66.66%><div
class="wp-block-group alignfull has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained" style=padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><h1 class="wp-block-post-title">Project Manager, Inclusive Livestock Development for Smallholders Farmers (“INCLUDE”) Jobs – SNV</h1><div
class="wp-block-group has-link-color has-accent-4-color has-text-color has-small-font-size is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-4efaea1e wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style=margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><p>This job falls under:</p><div
style=font-weight:300 class="taxonomy-category wp-block-post-terms"><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/communications-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Communications Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/information-technology-it-and-data-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Information Technology (IT) and Data Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/sales-and-marketing-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Sales and Marketing Jobs in Uganda</a></div></div><div
class="entry-content alignfull wp-block-post-content has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-post-content-is-layout-constrained"><div
class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; background-color: FFFFFF;'><div
align=center> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script> 
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=7510899927
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div></div><p><strong>Job Title: <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ > Project Manager, Inclusive Livestock Development for Smallholders Farmers (“INCLUDE”)</a></strong></p><p><strong>Organisation:</strong> SNV</p><p><strong>Duty Station:</strong> Fort Portal, Uganda</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>About Organisation: </strong></p><p>SNV is an international development organisation that applies practical know-how to make a lasting difference in the lives of people living in poverty. We use our extensive and long-term in-country presence to apply and adapt our expertise in agriculture, energy and WASH to local contexts. SNV has annual revenues of over €120 million, and 1300 staff working in 25 countries across Asia, Africa and Latin America. We are proud to be a not-for-profit organisation that uses project financing to implement our mission.</p><p></p><p><strong>Job Summary: </strong> As the Project Manager for the INCLUDE project under SNV Uganda’s Agri-Food Sector, you will lead the implementation of a transformative 5-year initiative aimed at improving the living income and building resilient livestock-based livelihoods for 75,000 smallholder farmer households across the Busoga, Rwenzori, Greater Ankole, and Kigezi subregions. Based full-time in Fort Portal, Uganda, this pivotal role requires a dynamic leader with a strong grasp of inclusive development and systems thinking to navigate complex rural ecosystems and drive sustainable change.</p><p>The INCLUDE project focuses on two key outcome areas: sustainable livestock production and inclusive market development. Through the Participatory Integrated Planning (PIP) approach, you will guide farming communities to strengthen their adaptive capacities, optimize land use, increase productivity, and access better markets and nutrition. Your leadership will ensure local ownership of solutions and meaningful farmer engagement.</p><p>Reporting to the Sector Leader, Agri-Food Sector, SNV Uganda, you will oversee a team of 32 dedicated staff and serve as the primary liaison with the donor (EKN). Your role will be instrumental in aligning project delivery with donor priorities, ensuring high-quality implementation, rigorous reporting, and strong stakeholder collaboration throughout the life of the project.</p><p></p><p><strong>Key Duties and Responsibilities: </strong></p><p><strong><em>Strategic Project Leadership and Technical Oversight of project implementation</em></strong></p><ul>
<li>Provide overall strategic direction for the INCLUDE project, ensuring full alignment with SNV’s agri-food systems approach and donor priorities as well compliance and accountability towards all SNV policies and procedures.</li>
<li>Guide the implementation of project pathways with a quality and learning lens: Ensuring timely, high-quality project delivery against scope and secure budget planning, expenditure tracking, and compliance with required SNV documentation.</li>
<li>Lead adaptively with focus on quality assurance and learning with data and through periodic reflection, consultation, and reporting in collaboration with EKN and peer initiatives (MEL).</li>
<li>Offer technical advisory to staff and partners, troubleshoot potential challenges and promote evidence-based decision making and continuous improvement of project delivery.</li></ul><p><strong><em>Team Leadership and Staff Development</em></strong></p><ul>
<li>Lead, coach, and mentor a diverse team of 32 development professionals, promoting a collaborative learning culture with the aim to deliver goals and objectives.</li>
<li>Lead recruitment, performance and staff development to ensure the right skillsets and mindsets across the team to support and enable empowerment.</li>
<li>Ensure that staff wellbeing and safety according to SNV code of conduct and related policies.</li></ul><p><strong><em>Stakeholder Engagement and Partnership Management</em></strong></p><ul>
<li>Serve as the primary liaison with the donor (EKN), fostering a transparent and pro-active relationship through regular updates and consultations.</li>
<li>Coordinate and collaborate closely with implementing partners, government institutions, civil society actors, and private sector stakeholders to ensure strong collaboration and alignment.</li>
<li>Proactively build linkages with other food security initiatives to maximize synergy and scale development outcomes.</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>Qualifications, Skills and Experience:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><ul>
<li>Master’s degree in Agriculture, Business, Livestock development, Economics, Rural Development, or a related field relevant to agri-food systems transformation.</li>
<li>Minimum of 10 years of progressive leadership experience managing complex, multi-stakeholder development programs in the agri-food or livestock sector (preferably in sub-Saharan Africa) to ensure improved livelihoods and food security.</li>
<li>Proven ability to mobilize, inspire, lead and guide multidisciplinary teams, enabling performance and impact through effective planning, delivery oversight, and adaptive management.</li>
<li>Track record of coaching and developing towards high-performing teams, with a commitment to capability -growth, well-being, and promoting inclusive, value-based leadership.</li>
<li>Strong stakeholder engagement and donor coordination experience, including successfully aligning public and private sector partnerships for systems-level impact.</li></ul><p><strong><em>Preferred Qualifications:</em></strong></p><ul>
<li>Postgraduate qualification or certification in Project Management, Organizational Leadership or related discipline that reinforces structured delivery and team leadership.</li>
<li>Experience leading through complexity, using evidence-based decision-making, continuous learning, and knowledge sharing to navigate systemic challenges and drive innovation.</li>
<li>Demonstrate expertise in inclusive market systems, livestock value chains, or climate-resilient agricultural systems, including participatory planning tools such as Participatory Integrated Planning (PIP).</li>
<li>Excellent coalition-building and influencing skills, with experience fostering cross-sector collaboration that results in or exceeds planned scalable and sustainable development results.</li>
<li>Extensive experience engaging with private sector actors, fostering investment in smallholder development, and brokering impactful partnerships that result in sustainable, scalable solutions.</li>
<li>Familiarity with Uganda’s agricultural policy landscape and rural institutions systems, with an ability to build trust and alignment with local and national stakeholders.</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>How to Apply:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><p>If you believe that your credentials meet the outlined profile, we invite you to apply by uploading your CV and motivation letter in English.</p><p></p><p><a
href=https://jobs.smartrecruiters.com/SNV/744000080139349-project-manager-inclusive-livestock-development-for-smallholders-farmers-include- rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank><strong>Click Here</strong></a></p><p></p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>Deadline: 21st September 2025</strong></p><p></p><p>  </p><p></p><p>For more of the latest jobs, please visit <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ >https://www.theugandanjobline.com</a> or find us on our facebook page <a
href=https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank>https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline</a></p><p> </p><p></p><p>Level of Education: Postgraduate Degree</p><p>Work Hours: 8</p><p>Experience in Months: 120</p><p><script type=application/ld+json>{"@context":"https://schema.org/","@type":"JobPosting","title":"Project Manager, Inclusive Livestock Development for Smallholders Farmers - Fort Portal","description":"Job Summary:   As the Project Manager for the INCLUDE project under SNV Uganda\u2019s Agri-Food Sector, you will lead the implementation of a transformative 5-year initiative aimed at improving the living income and building resilient livestock-based livelihoods for 75,000 smallholder farmer households across the Busoga, Rwenzori, Greater Ankole, and Kigezi subregions. class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-28f84493 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex"><div
class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style=flex-basis:66.66%><div
class="wp-block-group alignfull has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained" style=padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><h1 class="wp-block-post-title">Transport and Logistics Officer &#8211; Locum Jobs – Joint Clinical Research Centre (JCRC)</h1><div
class="wp-block-group has-link-color has-accent-4-color has-text-color has-small-font-size is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-4efaea1e wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style=margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60)><p>This job falls under:</p><div
style=font-weight:300 class="taxonomy-category wp-block-post-terms"><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/procurement-and-logistics-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Procurement and Logistics Jobs in Uganda</a><span
class=wp-block-post-terms__separator>, </span><a
href=https://theugandanjobline.com/category/transport-and-driver-jobs-in-uganda rel=tag>Transport and Driver Jobs in Uganda</a></div></div><div
class="entry-content alignfull wp-block-post-content has-global-padding is-layout-constrained wp-block-post-content-is-layout-constrained"><div
class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; background-color: FFFFFF;'><div
align=center> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script> 
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=7510899927
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div></div><p><strong>Job Title: </strong><a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ ><strong> Transport and Logistics Officer &#8211; Locum     </strong></a></p><p><strong>Organisation: </strong>Joint Clinical Research Centre (JCRC)</p><p><strong>Duty Station: </strong>Mbarara<strong>, </strong>Uganda</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>About Organisation:</strong></p><p>The Joint Clinical Research Centre (JCRC) is an indigenous medical organization that was established in 1991 as a limited liability not-for-profit Joint-venture between the Uganda Ministry of Health (MoH), Ministry of Defense and Makerere University Medical School (now Makerere University College of Health Sciences). JCRC is located on plot 101 Lubowa Hill Off Entebbe Road P.O. Box 10005 Kampala.</p><p> </p><p></p><p><strong>Job Summary: </strong> Manage and control the effective use of organization&#8217;s vehicles to ensure good stewardship as per JCRC and Donor Transport Policy and Procedures to ensure that fleet is maintained in the manner that will provide reliable transportation for effective implementation of project work.</p><p></p><p><strong>Key Duties and Responsibilities: </strong></p><ul>
<li>Facilitate the registration of Motor Vehicles, renewal of Road Licenses and Fitness.</li>
<li>Maintain the Vehicle Database for proper review and monitoring.</li>
<li>Ensure the issuance of a weekly travel matrix.</li>
<li>Produce summary of vehicle usage reports.</li>
<li>Scheduling &amp; Routing of vehicles &amp; drivers to ensure that members of staff needing transport are facilitated to carry out their various assignments. </li>
<li>Facilitate healthy functioning and timely service of all vehicles and ensuring that all repairs carried out meet the required standard to minimize accidents and break downs.</li>
<li>Ensure that comprehensive Insurance for all Motor vehicle/bikes is done and insurance claims are affected immediately after the accident has occurred.</li>
<li>Be available 24hrs to aid in case of accidents or breakdowns and to effect emergence repairs by ensuring that there is appropriate security for project motor vehicles.</li>
<li>Ensure that appropriate procedures and control on the issuance of fuel and lubricants is in place.</li>
<li>Monitoring of vehicle movements through the tracking system as per standard procedures.</li>
<li>Provide project vehicle logbooks to document and monitor vehicle transport utilization as per required JCRC standards and systems.</li>
<li>Prepare monthly comparative analysis reports to ensure that fuel drawn on all vehicles &amp; motorbikes to good use.</li>
<li>Work in liaison with Supply Chain in recommending standard models of motor vehicles/bikes that meet required operational needs.</li>
<li>Provide supervision and identify training gaps to drivers.</li>
<li>Participate and support development and design of guidelines/policies that relate to fleet for JCRC for effective operations.</li>
<li>Review of the accountability documentation from hired vehicles, garages, washing bays and other related</li>
<li>Undertake additional assignments given by immediate supervisor.</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>Qualifications, Skills and Experience:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><ul>
<li>The applicant must hold a Bachelors-level education/training or equivalent experience in Finance and Business Management or related technical fields.</li>
<li>At least five (5) years of experience working on USG-funded projects, PEPFAR funding and reporting, and/or public health programs highly desirable.</li>
<li>Demonstrated interest in and experience in organizational or individual capacity building and/or training.</li>
<li>Experience with US Government-funded projects and acquisition and assistance rules and regulations.</li>
<li>Demonstrated knowledge of granting procedures, from grant start-up, award management, to close out.</li>
<li>Demonstrated competence to assess priorities and manage a variety of activities in a time-sensitive environment and meet deadlines with attention to detail and quality.</li>
<li>Demonstrated attention to detail, ability to implement procedures, meet deadlines and work independently and cooperatively with team members.</li>
<li>Ability to work independently, take initiative and manage various activities in a team setting with minimal supervision.</li>
<li>Experience developing contracts and managing an acquisition process to completion.</li>
<li>Strong time management/task prioritization skills.</li>
<li>Computer literacy required (especially Excel, MS Word and Windows).</li>
<li>Strong communication and interpersonal skills.</li>
<li>A proven ability to work as part of a team and to be self-managing</li></ul><p></p><p><strong>How to Apply:</p><div
style="text-align:center; margin:20px 0;"> <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-9951482434865458"
     crossorigin=anonymous></script><br>
<br>
<ins
class=adsbygoogle
style=display:block
data-ad-client=ca-pub-9951482434865458
data-ad-slot=9585539503
data-ad-format=auto
data-full-width-responsive=true></ins><br> <script>(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({});</script> </div><p> </strong></p><p>All applications should be addressed to; The Head Human Resources, Joint Clinical Research Centre, Plot 101 Lubowa Campus off Entebbe Road, P.O Box 10005, Kampala-Uganda via Email at <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="147e7b7667547e7766777b66733a6173">[email&#160;protected]</a>. Applicants are STRICTLY advised to apply with a cover letter and CV combined in one PDF document not exceeding six pages.</p><p></p><p><strong>Deadline: 15th, August 2025</strong></p><p></p><p><strong>NB:</strong> Failure to follow instructions while applying will automatically lead to disqualification. Only shortlisted candidates will be contacted. Successful applicants will be required to start immediately after appropriate screening checks.</p><p></p><p>For more of the latest jobs, please visit <a
href=https://www.theugandanjobline.com/ >https://www.theugandanjobline.com</a> or find us on our facebook page <a
href=https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline rel="nofollow noopener" target=_blank>https://www.facebook.com/UgandanJobline</a></p><p></p><p>Level of Education: Bachelor Degree</p><p>Work Hours: 8</p><p>Experience in Months: 60</p></p><p><script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script
